</span><span class="cl-9152aab8">crisis</span><span class="cl-9152aaa4"> </span><span class="cl-9152aaa4">about</span><span class="cl-9152aaa4"> </span><span class="cl-9152aab8">sentence</span><span latter half of June 1951.</span></p></td><td class="cl-91733d1f"><p class="cl-917312a8"><span class="cl-91730772">India</span><span class="cl-9173075e"> </span><span propaganda that is daily growing in volume in Pakistan which justify the suspicion that they are part of a planned program calculated to lead, if unchecked, to an outbreak of hostilities between the two countries."</span></p></td><td class="cl-91733d14"><p class="cl-917312a8"><span class="cl-9173075e">No</span><span class="cl-9173075e"> </span><span India.</span></p></td><td class="cl-91733d1f"><p class="cl-917312a8"><span class="cl-91730772">Pakistan</span><span class="cl-9173075e"> </span><span class="cl-9173075e">initiated</span><span strictly economic grounds.</span></p></td><td class="cl-91a9ba7f"><p class="cl-91a99512"><span class="cl-91a989e6">German</span><span class="cl-91a989e6"> </span><span
